Fleas in Shandong

[Special Dispatch from This Newspaper, Nanjing, 26th] When the National Army was approaching Yingxi County, Shandong, a Wang couple in the city whispered while going to bed: "The Central Army is coming soon!" The next day, the couple was arrested. The bandit army tied their thumbs with ropes and hung them high in the treetops for interrogation: "Now let you see the Central Army!" Then they cut the ropes and shot them dead on the spot. This crime and punishment is called "Looking at the Central Army".

This matter was told to the reporter by He Zhihao, a battlefield inspector specially appointed by the Chairman of the National Government. He was dispatched to inspect the Shandong war zone and has been in the front line for two months. He told reporters that before the National Army captured Feicheng, the communist bandits convened a mass meeting to discuss a proposal to burn the entire village.

When the villagers raised their hands to vote, the chairman declared: "The Communist Party is democratic and wants to seek everyone's consent before doing something. Now we want to burn the houses. Does everyone agree?" The crowd was terrified and did not answer. The chairman said again: "The Communist Party is the most democratic. Burning houses must be approved by everyone's opinion!" The crowd was even more terrified, looking at each other in silence. At this time, the chairman turned red, stared, and shouted sternly: "The Communist Party is the most democratic. Burning houses is also for the benefit of the people. The people's affairs must be agreed to by the people, but the thoughts of older people are always backward. Let's see what the opinions of the new forces, the children, are!" So, the "Children's Team" raised their hands in favor, and it was passed as a majority. This is an example of the Communist Party's "democracy". If the ancient Greek philosophers who created the political theory of democracy knew that the Chinese Communist Party today practices "democracy" in this way, they would definitely laugh and cry!

"Dividing the houses" is a seductive slogan. The poor were delighted when they first heard it, but the communist bandits had a strange way of "equalizing wealth": the masses gathered in front of the mansion, and after a meeting and vote, the houses were immediately demolished. The target of the liquidation became a pile of rubble. The masses who struggled were divided into broken bricks and broken pillars. The communist bandits had completed another act of destruction. This kind of "equalization of wealth" has caused the tragedy of ten cities out of ten empty in many towns in Shandong.

What the people fear most is the communist bandit's census.

Before the census, the bandits sent spies into the houses in advance. At night, the census team fought outside and shouted, "Check the household registration!" If the family wanted to hide a strong man or hide some food, the bandit hiding in the house would see everything clearly, and the result would inevitably be severe punishment.

A certain division commander stationed in the Yimeng Mountain area said when entertaining the inspectors: "You have been bumping around on the front line, contacting only soldiers. Now I will give you a little adjustment and ask you to take a look at the women!" Sure enough, the guards were ordered to bring a woman. Everyone looked at her and almost vomited. It was a Russian old woman captured by the division from the bandit army.

She wore a Chinese cheongsam, covered in dirt, with no expression on her face. No matter how you questioned her, she didn't say a word. Old, ugly, and disgusting, she was like a witch in a Grimm's fairy tale. Searching her body for documents, it was known that she had been active in the Northeast. If she really couldn't speak Chinese, she must have had a translator working for the bandit army, and there must be more than just one Russian!

In the captured bandit army's battle order, there was a paragraph: "Fight with what gun you have, fight against what enemy, fight at what time and place." It seems that Chen Yi, that fellow, only specializes in fighting messy battles.

The National Army's Russian woman captured from the bandit army in the Yimeng Mountain area (sent by Shaochuan)

His main force has been looking for the weakness of the National Army, trying to harvest the effect of annihilation in mobile warfare, but the communist party's sugar-coated poison pill has been fed to the people of Shandong, and it has ruined its own political life. The people in the "liberated areas" don't want you! They are not afraid of you using the severe torture of "Looking at the Central Army". They still want the Central Army! The folk song "Down with Mao Zedong, everyone will have merit" hit the mark. Coupled with the advance of the loyal and brave National Army, dozens of dark "liberated area" towns and villages have been restored. Now, the remaining bandits in the border areas can only act as flea-like harassment, and it will not be difficult to clear them in the short term. (Special Correspondent Hang Shaochuan)

Case of Zou Yue'e from Wujiang Raped to Death - Full Text of the Judgment

[Our Nanjing 27th Dispatch] Liu Keming and four other principal offenders in the case of Zou Yue'e, a female student at Tongli Town National Elementary School in Wujiang, who was raped to death and robbed of her belongings, were sentenced to death by the Military Law Department of the Ministry of National Defense today and executed by firing squad. The full text of the judgment is as follows:

Judgment of the Ministry of National Defense - Original Copy

Defendant Liu Keming (male, 31 years old, from Ziyang County, Sichuan Province, formerly a member of the 29th Army Officer Training Corps, now retired).

Zhou Tianquan (male, 42 years old, from Anyue County, Sichuan Province, Captain of the Fourth Platoon of the Seventeenth Team of the 29th Army Officer Training Corps).

Pu Yuzhou (male, 31 years old, from Ba County, Sichuan Province, formerly a member of the 29th Army Officer Training Corps, now retired).

Peng Hengda (male, 28 years old, from Tongliang County, Sichuan Province, formerly a member of the 29th Army Officer Training Corps, now retired).

Zhang Shaoyun (also known as Zhang Shaoyun, male, formerly a member of the 29th Army Officer Training Corps, now retired).

Liu Guozhang (male, 38 years old, from Shehong County, Sichuan Province, formerly a member of the 29th Army Officer Training Corps, now retired).

Liu Jun (male, 30 years old, from Chongqing City, Sichuan Province, formerly a member of the 29th Army Officer Training Corps, now retired).

Zhang Yishou (male, 38 years old, from Lezhi County, Sichuan Province, formerly a member of the 29th Army Officer Training Corps, now retired).

Pu Pan Shi (female, 30 years old, from Fanchang County, Anhui Province).

The judgment of this Ministry in the case of the above-mentioned defendants for robbery and other circumstances is as follows:

Main Text:

Liu Keming is sentenced to death for jointly robbing and intentionally killing, and is deprived of public rights for life.

Zhou Tianquan is sentenced to death for colluding to rob, and is deprived of public rights for life.

Pu Yuzhou is sentenced to death for jointly robbing and intentionally killing, and is deprived of public rights for life. He is sentenced to death for selling drugs and is deprived of public rights for life. The death sentence will be carried out, and he is deprived of public rights for life.

Peng Hengda and Zhang Shaoyun (also known as Zhang Shaoyun) are each sentenced to death for jointly robbing and intentionally killing, and are each deprived of public rights for life.

Liu Guozhang, Liu Jun, Zhang Yishou, and Pu Pan Shi are all innocent.

Facts:

Liu Keming, Pu Yuzhou, Peng Hengda, and Zhang Shaoyun were all members of the 29th Army Officer Training Corps. They retired successively between April and May of this year and stayed in Wujiang County, Jiangsu Province, where they organized a gang. Pu Yuzhou, carrying his family, resided in the home of Zou Wu Shi at No. 5 West Bank, Tongli Town, Wujiang County, making a living by selling drugs. He knew that the Chen family next door was relatively well-off, that her husband had passed away, and that her sons and nephews were doing business elsewhere. The Chen family consisted only of Chen and her daughter Zou Yue'e, and they were isolated and unable to resist. Pu Yuzhou then conspired with Liu, Peng, Zhang, and Zhou Tianquan, a member of the 17th Company of the 5th Battalion of the Training Corps, to carry out a robbery. They planned that on the afternoon of June 4th of this year, at about 4:00 PM, Liu Keming would go to the Zou residence, falsely claiming to be unable to find a house to rent, and deposit his luggage there, as a pretext for entering the house at night. The Chen mother and daughter were suspicious and asked their cousin Zou Bingcheng to stay with them that night. That night at around 9:00 PM, Liu Keming, Zhou Tianquan, Pu Yuzhou, Peng Hengda, Zhang Shaoyun, Peng Ming, Li Pengyun, Chen Lizhong, [blank] Jia, Hu Zhan [blank] Liao Bingming and others, carrying guns, went to carry out the plan, claiming to retrieve the luggage. The Zou residence fell into their trap and opened the gate. The bandits successively rushed in five people, Peng Hengda jumped over the wall into the inner room. The gang immediately forced Zou Bingcheng to call out to open the second door, and Pu Hengda and Tong Tianquan and others bound Chen's daughter and Zou Bingcheng and his wife together. Because Zou Yue'e shouted for help, Liu used a yardstick to push cotton into her mouth, and then raped her, causing Yue'e to suffocate and die. The [blank] and others robbed the Chen family of seven gold rings and one gold bracelet, and Zou Bingcheng of one gold ring, before fleeing. Zou Chen reported the incident to the Wujiang District Prosecutor's Office, which verified that Zou Yue'e had been raped before death and suffocated, as recorded in the files. The 29th Army Officer Training Corps, upon receiving the report, together with the mayor of Tongli Town, arrested Tong Tianquan, Pu Yuzhou, Peng Hengda, Zhang Shaoyun, Liu Keming, and suspects Pu Pan Shi, Liu Guozhang, Liu Jun, Zhang Yi [blank] and others and escorted them to the case.

The Five Executed Criminals: Liu Keming, Pu Yuzhou, Peng Hengda, Zhang Shaoyun, Zhou Tianquan.

The reasons for this case are described in detail below:

(A) Regarding Liu Keming, Pu Yuzhou, Zhou Tianquan, Peng Hengda, and Zhang Shaoyun: Although the defendants were cunning and did not confess to the facts listed on the right, the files show that Zhou Tianquan confessed in the Officer Training Corps: "That day it was almost dark, I ran into Liu Keming on the bridge, and then I met Pu Yuzhou, Peng Hengda, Zhang Shaoyun, Peng Ming, etc. We went to the Zou family together. Liu Keming called the door, and an old grandmother opened the door. Everyone went in. We ran into the old lady, Liu Keming looked for Zou Yue'e, first he argued with her, and then he punched her. She ran away, and Liu also followed her in. Peng Hengda and Liu Keming tied her up. Pu Yuzhou and Zhang Shaoyun stood at the door, and the rest stood in the courtyard. Liu Keming held her down (referring to the deceased) and used a ruler to shove cotton in her mouth" (see Officer Training Corps file, June 11th record). Liu Keming confessed: "On June 3rd, at Pu Yuzhou's house, Pu said that the Zou family didn't have many people, and they had a lot of gold and cash. We could go and do a job and make some money. On the morning of the 4th, we planned to do it at night. We gathered at the entrance of Pu's house. Two people from Tongli each brought guns. Li Pengju, Fan Qikui, and Ran Qixi and I also brought guns. There was probably a lock set inside" (see Officer Training Corps investigation file, June 12th record). Pu Yuzhou confessed: "Liu Keming brought the quilt in. He used the excuse of putting the quilt down so that he could go at night. Liu Keming and Zhang Shaoyun were the ones who kicked the door open and went in. They told me that they were going to rob the Zou family tonight. I replied that they shouldn't hurt anyone. They told me to look at the back door. Zou Yue'e shouted loudly, and Liu Keming stuffed her mouth with cotton," etc. (see Officer Training Corps file, June 12th record). Questioning the plaintiff, Zou Chen Shi, she stated: "They first tied my daughter in the room for half an hour. One of them came out, wiping his sweat, it looked like him (referring to Liu Keming), the one who brought the bedding during the day, and the one who came over from Pu's side door first, it was also him. This person (referring to Zhou Tianquan) tied me up and asked me for money and gold." Zou Shen Shi, the deceased Zou Yue'e's sister-in-law, stated: "That day at two o'clock, [blank] from the Pu family came over, I opened the door, the one who entered the [blank] house was him" (referring to Liu Keming) (see Wujiang District Court file, page 69). Jin Shan Quan (also known as Jin Xiaosu, the deceased's nephew) stated: "That night he (referring to Zhou Tianquan) tied up my grandmother and stuffed cotton in her mouth, that's absolutely correct." Further investigation of Pu Yuzhou's drug dealing, Zou Wu Shi (Pu's landlord) stated: "Many people came and went to Pu's house. At night, I smelled a scent, a white powder scent (i.e., heroin). [Blank] three often came and went. I had eaten it for a few days when I was thirty years old, so I smelled the white powder" (see court file, page 63). Peng Hengda confessed: "Someone surnamed Ran said that he had white flour to buy at his house. Liu Keming confessed: "The one who runs the white flour business in Tongli Hall told me that his family sells white flour" (see record of joint trial by this Ministry). Although Peng Hengda vehemently denied being involved in the robbery and claimed that he had already returned home that night and had not gone out, and that the landlord opened the door, which could serve as proof to the contrary, Peng's landlord Xue Shen Shi stated: "Peng went out after dark that night and didn't come back until 11:00." Moreover, Zou Bingcheng pointed out: "There are two Zhang Shaoyuns there, I am numbers three, four, and five, living at number 22, Jincheng Hotel, Suzhou, and numbers 6, staying at the garrison of the 145th Division in Laolumen" (see the original file of the town office), and also called the orderly Tian Yun at the garrison (see file [blank] page 28). After detailed verification of the Jincheng Hotel's log, there was no registration of Zhang Shaoyun staying there, and the garrison of the 145th Division had no person named Tian Yun (see Wujiang County Government telegram of August 19). Zhang Yixun stated: "The Zhang Shaoyun who lives in Zhenze is very old, and I watched a play with him at the Zhenze Theater on the evening of June 4th." Pu Yuzhou stated: "This Zhang Shaoyun was definitely captured" (see court file, page 38), etc. The evidence to the contrary presented by Peng Hengda and Zhang Shaoyun is insufficient to prove their claims. Furthermore, they have been clearly identified by the victims and accomplices, so their empty words of sophistry and denial of responsibility cannot be accepted. After reviewing the entire file, the defendants either confessed frankly, or were clearly identified by the victims, and the evidence corroborates each other. They are all principals in the commission of the crime, and there is no doubt about it. Considering their actions, Zhou Tianquan is a soldier and should be convicted of colluding to rob. The deceased Zou Yue'e was verified to have been raped, and it was Liu Keming who dragged her to the ground in the hall, and left only after half an hour. It is extremely clear that Liu is the principal offender in the rape, and he should be convicted of both robbery resulting in intentional homicide and robbery resulting in rape. However, because these acts arose from a single act of robbery, the more serious charge of jointly robbing and intentionally killing should be applied. Pu Yuzhou, Peng Hengda, and Zhang Shaoyun should be convicted of jointly robbing and intentionally killing. Furthermore, Pu Yuzhou sold drugs, which has been corroborated by multiple testimonies and is therefore reliable. He should be convicted of selling drugs. These charges should be considered separately and punished concurrently with the charge of jointly robbing and intentionally killing, as the intent of each crime is different.

(B) Regarding Liu Guozhang, Liu Jun, Zhang Yishou, and Pu Pan Shi: After repeated investigations of Liu Guozhang, Liu Jun, Zhang Yishou, and Pu Pan Shi, they have all vehemently denied participating in the robbery. Neither the victims nor the principals Liu Keming, Zhou Tianquan, and Pu Yuzhou have implicated them as accomplices. It should be considered that the evidence of their guilt is insufficient to prove their involvement in the crime, and they should all be found not guilty.

Based on the above conclusions, in accordance with Article 2, Item 5 of the Provisional Emergency Military and Political Measures for the Pacification Zone and the Nine Northeastern Provinces, Article 1, Article 2, the first paragraph of Article 8 of the Wartime Army, Navy, and Air Force Summary Trial Regulations, Article 291 of the Code of Criminal Procedure, the first paragraph of Article 293, Article 84, Article 15 of the Army, Navy, and Air Force Criminal Law, Article 2, Item 1, Clause 6 and Clause 8, Article 9 and Article 51, Clause 1 and Clause 8, Article 37, Clause 1 of the Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits, judgment is rendered as stated in the main text. August, 1936 of the Republic of China. Joint deliberation and judgment by Presiding Judge Zhang [blank] Sheng, Judge Liu Mengjiu, and Du Mulu.

Regulations for Commending Donations to Education - The Ministry of Education Revised and the National Government Approved and Promulgated the Full Text of Fourteen Articles, Awarding Prizes Based on Seven Standards

[Our Nanjing 28th Dispatch] The Ministry of Education revised the Regulations for Commending Donations to Education this summer, which have recently been approved and promulgated by the National Government. These are quite different from those revised in 1934. "Regulations for Commending Donations to Education": (Article 1) Private individuals or organizations who donate to public or registered private schools, libraries, museums, art galleries, gymnasiums, public education centers, or other educational or cultural professionals shall be given commendations in accordance with these Regulations. Foreigners who donate to education may be commended in accordance with these Regulations. (Article 2) The methods of commendation are as follows: Certificates of merit are divided into four grades and are given by the provincial government or the [blank] municipal government. Medals are divided into gold and silver, and are given by the Ministry of Education. Plaques are given by the National Government. (Article 3) The standards for awarding donations are as follows: A donation of 300,000 yuan or more but less than 500,000 yuan will be given a fourth-grade certificate of merit. A donation of 500,000 yuan or more but less than 1,000,000 yuan will be given a third-grade certificate of merit. A donation of 1,000,000 yuan or more but less than 2,000,000 yuan will be given a second-grade certificate of merit. A donation of 2,000,000 yuan or more but less than 5,000,000 yuan will be given a first-grade certificate of merit. A donation of 5,000,000 yuan or more but less than 10,000,000 yuan will be given a silver [blank] medal. A donation of 10,000,000 yuan or more but less than 50,000,000 yuan will be given a gold [blank] medal. A donation of 50,000,000 yuan or more will be given a plaque. (Article 4) For those who should be given awards in accordance with Article 3 of these Regulations, the competent official [blank] shall issue a statement of facts, attach donation certificates, and the recipient's resume, and submit it to the provincial government or the directly subordinate municipal government for verification and awarding. At the end of the year, the provincial and municipal governments shall report [blank] to the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of the Interior for record. (Article 5) Those who should be awarded medals in accordance with the provisions of Article 3 of these Regulations shall have the competent authorities issue a statement of facts, attach donation certificates, and the recipient's resume, and submit it to the higher-level authorities, which will send it to the Ministry of Education, together with the Ministry of the Interior, for verification and submission to the Executive Yuan for approval, and then the Ministry of Education will award the medals. (Article 6) For those who should be given plaques in accordance with the provisions of Article 3 of these Regulations, the competent authorities shall state the facts, attach donation certificates, and the recipient's resume, and submit it to the higher-level authorities, which will send it to the Ministry of Education, after consultation with the Ministry of the Interior, for submission to the Executive Yuan, which will then submit it to the National Government for awarding. (Article 7) Chinese citizens residing [blank] abroad who should be given commendations in accordance with Article 3 of these Regulations shall have the local embassy or consulate issue a statement of facts, attach donation certificates, and the recipient's resume, and report it to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, together with the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of the Interior, for handling. In places where there are no embassies or consulates, the principal or chairman of the school board or other responsible person for overseas Chinese education may submit it to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for verification and then, together with the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of the Interior, award the commendation. (Article 8) Donations in Mongolia and Tibet shall be awarded separately by the League and Banner authorities in Mongolia and the local authorities in Tibet in accordance with the provisions of these Regulations, and shall be reported to the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of the Interior, and the Mongolian [blank] Committee for record at the end of the year. (Article 9) Those who have already received a certificate of merit or medal and continue to donate or donate in two or more places, the total amount of donations will be added to award prizes, limited to one time, and one person shall not be given two kinds of certificates of merit or medals at the same time. (Article 10) Those who raise donations exceeding ten times the amount listed in each item of Article 3 of these Regulations may be commended in accordance with the provisions of the same article, but those whose fundraising is part of their job duties shall not be subject to the provisions of these Regulations. (Article 11) Donations made in real estate or movable property other than national currency shall be converted into national currency based on the local market price. (Article 12) The awarding of commendations to foreigners shall be handled by the Ministry of Education, together with the Ministry of the Interior and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. (Article 13) The designs of plaques, certificates of merit, and medals shall be determined by the Ministry of the Interior. (Article 14) These Regulations shall come into force from the date of promulgation.

Opinions on Hu Shih's Ten-Year Education Plan by Cheng Hsiaogang

Each school has its own unique strengths. The dentistry of West China University and the agriculture of Nanking University are strengths not possessed by Peking University and the other four. In developing academic pursuits, one should focus on these special departments and assist their development, so that they can achieve first-class international academic status.

[Our Newspaper's Report] Cheng Hsiaogang, the new president of Jiaotong University, arrived in Shanghai the other day and stayed at the Yangzi Telegraph Office Guesthouse. He is scheduled to take office at the university this morning.

Mr. Cheng, in response to questions from reporters at the guesthouse yesterday, stated the following: Since the end of the war, the number of faculty and students at Jiaotong University has increased dramatically. The existing facilities have been unable to keep up with the current needs, which has had a significant impact on teaching and learning. Everyone shares this sentiment. This individual is now in charge of the university administration and is eager to gain cooperation and assistance from all sides in developing the university's affairs in the future, focusing on concrete actions. It is futile to engage in empty talk at this time without immediate results. However, I can say that both myself and others connected to Jiaotong University hope to restore the university's previous high academic standards in the short term, enhance the students' desire for learning. The Ministry of Education has already increased the number of professors by more than a hundred this semester. The equipment donated by the United Nations Relief and Rehabilitation Administration (UNRRA) will also be very helpful for teaching experiments. In terms of funding, in addition to the Ministry of Education, we have also approached various parties for donations, hoping to improve the welfare of faculty and students as much as possible. As for the various matters already decided by the Jiaotong University Reorganization Committee, Mr. Cheng stated that he would not make any changes. Mr. Cheng then expressed his opinion on the ten-year education plan of Hu Shih, the president of Peking University, saying that universities include a wide range of departments, and each school has its own unique strengths. The dentistry of West China University and the agriculture of Nanking University are strengths not possessed by Peking University and the other four. In developing academic pursuits, one should focus on these special departments and assist their development, so that they can achieve first-class international academic status, and one name cannot replace its position. He believes that the division of labor in science is becoming increasingly detailed and beneficial. In agricultural studies, there is the field of botany, and within botany, there are the departments of plant diseases and entomology. For example, the cotton produced in Dali, Yunnan, is of very good quality, growing taller than a person, but it is often damaged by pests and diseases, preventing large-scale production. In other areas, the losses caused by pests and diseases to our country's annual cotton, wheat, and rice production are countless, yet no one pays attention to researching prevention and control measures, which is very regrettable. Speaking of engineering, the division of labor is also detailed, and the achievements of various schools vary. The government should develop them separately based on the strengths of each school. Mr. Cheng hopes to replace Hu Shih's ten-year education plan with this idea. He pointed out: This can build on the existing foundation of each school, making it easier for greater development and allowing universities to compete with each other. It can also equalize funding and avoid regional disputes.

Group A Volleyball League: Yongsha Wins the Championship; Huayan Loses After a Five-Set Battle

[Our Newspaper's Report] Following the GuoZhen Cup, the Yongsha volleyball team has won the Group A championship in the second Volleyball League. They achieved six wins in six matches. In last night's final, they once again defeated Huayan in a dramatic five-set battle. After falling behind 1-2, Yongsha quickly rallied, winning two consecutive sets to come from behind and secure a 3-2 victory, which is highly gratifying. Huayan initially impressed, winning the first set and then taking a 2-1 lead. Unfortunately, in the extremely tense situation of the fourth set, when the score was tied at 19-19, they failed to seize the victory and allowed Yongsha to score two points, leading to a 21-19 score and a 2-2 tie, resulting in a decisive fifth set, which was a pity for Huayan. During the decisive fifth set, the atmosphere was tense. At first, the score was tied at 7-7 and 8-8, but Yongsha then pulled ahead with an 11-8 lead. As the score reached 17-11, Yongsha seemed destined to win. Huayan's ZhiJi served and scored four consecutive points, bringing the score to 17-15 and increasing the tension. Then, the score reached 19-17. Just when it seemed that Huayan could not rally, Yongsha scored two consecutive points to complete the victory. Last night, neither Yongsha nor Huayan showed any particularly outstanding performance, nor did Huayan seem destined to lose. The difference was slight.

The sporting ability last night was suddenly apparent, with about six or seven hundred people coming to watch the final. In the women's group, Fuhua defeated Jinde, and in the two Group B matches, Shangyu Huaqing won.

Tao Guanyu and McLagan Fail to Determine a Winner in the Semifinals; Mrs. Ye Guanziong Gains Right to the Women's Singles Final

[Our Newspaper's Report] Yesterday was the second day of the open tennis championship semi-finals. Textile Adjustment Committee Will Cooperate with Municipal Authorities to Crack Down on Yarn and Cloth Hoarding and Speculation, Starting with Inventory Checks and Registration

According to a statement by the person in charge of the Textile Adjustment Committee: The implementation plan for adjusting the supply and demand of yarn and cloth has been announced and implemented. In order to stabilize yarn prices, the committee has decided to severely crack down on hoarding and speculation of yarn and cloth based on this plan. The primary task is to conduct inventory checks of yarn and cloth on the market together with the municipal authorities, starting today. According to regulations, the amount of cotton yarn stored by each factory should be sufficient for three months of use by the factory. Yarn number storage shall not exceed forty-five days. Cloth merchants shall not store more than twice the amount of cloth they sell in their peak months. Overdue and excessive amounts will be seized and prosecuted as hoarding and speculation. The government will then purchase them at negotiated prices to suppress their illegal profits. Regarding the crackdown on speculative transactions in yarn and cloth, the Textile Adjustment Committee will dispatch personnel at any time together with the municipal government to secretly investigate the cotton yarn and cloth market. If any acts of monopoly, speculative buying and selling, or short selling are discovered, they will be reported and punished. The registration of cotton yarn and cloth inventory, the registration of cotton yarn and cloth businesses, and the registration of cotton yarn reproduction industries will be carried out separately.

Cotton Yarn Negotiated Pricing Method Extended to Tianjin, Hankou, and Guangzhou

In order to suppress cotton yarn prices, the Textile Adjustment Committee will extend the cotton yarn negotiated pricing method to Tianjin, Hankou, and Guangzhou. The committee will set up branches in the above three cities to handle matters according to Shanghai standards. For those transported via the Beijing-Shanghai route, transportation costs and profits will be added. If local producers are involved, prices will be negotiated with reference to local production costs and market conditions, and reported to the committee for record. This will be implemented in a short period of time.

Black Market Cannot Be Eliminated, Overseas Remittances Cannot Enter the Right Track

[Our Newspaper's Report] Relevant sources stated: The total amount of overseas remittances in July was over US$190,000. The statistics for August have not yet been compiled, but it is estimated that there will not be a significant increase or decrease. This figure is higher than before foreign exchange was listed, but it has not reached the expected hope. The key lies in the failure of the black market and the official exchange rate to align. Especially in areas close to our country, such as the Philippines and Southeast Asia, they are particularly sensitive to the difference between the black market and the official exchange rate. At the same time, the inflow of overseas remittances into the black market has become a habit, and it will not be possible to reverse this situation in a day. According to experts' estimates, before the war, 70% of our country's overseas remittances came from Southeast Asia and 30% from the United States and the United Kingdom. During the Pacific War, the entire territory of Southeast Asia fell, but our country's monthly overseas remittance income was still around US$10 million. If overseas remittances can be brought into the right track, the monthly amount could reach over US$40 million.

US Short-Term Treasury Bills Will Be Exchanged for Bonds Starting Today

Since their issuance, all of the sold US dollar short-term treasury bills have been subscription vouchers. It is now learned that the official treasury bills have been fully printed by the Ministry of Finance and have been fully allocated to the National Bank Treasury Bureau. The exchange will begin today. Those who have subscribed for treasury bill subscription vouchers can go directly to the original sales agency to exchange them.

Knitting and Talent Selection

— Ping

Qiu Ping and the knitting school have been around for a decade. Over the years, we have taught over a thousand students. Here, I will discuss some of my teaching experiences and my thoughts on talent selection:

Years of war caused the interruption of the wool industry. Consequently, knitting essentially came to a halt. Now, with the restoration of our nation, the wool industry has reached its peak in recent years. Since the start of autumn, newly opened yarn shops have sprung up like bamboo shoots after the rain, lined up on Jing'an Temple Road and Xiafei Road, as dense as stars in the sky. Thus, there is a great shortage of knitting talent. All of the students in the current 24th class have been hired to serve the community, providing free instruction to customers in order to achieve a thorough understanding of the art of knitting. However, the path to art is not limited to rigid and uninspired methods. It requires the selection of agile minds and the achievement of skills. Factors such as color coordination and the rules of contour rely on genius and wisdom, as well as continuous research, in order to achieve perfection. Therefore, the ladies who take on the role of knitting instructors must also examine their own cultivation, such as the effect of a warm and fulfilling personality! This includes gentle speech, graceful demeanor, and an upright appearance. However, this is not a necessary element among the conditions. As for respect for the shop owner and humility towards colleagues, it should be like a new bride's willingness to consider everything, maintaining an appropriate attitude and remaining a typical lady!

A Window-Shaped Short Outerwear by Sister Gu Lanjun

Description of the Window-Shaped Short Outerwear

— Qiu

Using the window-shaped flower to knit a woolen short jacket, from a distance it looks like a windowpane呢. We used two colors of wool yarn, knitting them apart, which further highlights its beauty. Because the window-shaped pattern has a convex round shape, whether knitting a window-shaped pattern has a style vest, travel outfit, more can take more ordinary tea, it is much better to look at.

Materials: 12 strands of fine yarn, 8 strands of light color, 4 strands of dark color

Tools: One set of single-pointed knitting needles, one set of double-pointed knitting needles, one embroidery needle

Start: Start with 110 stitches for 4 inches of 2 up and 2 down ribs on the side of the hem of the back panel, then knit the window-shaped pattern for one inch, and then increase at the waist, adding one stitch every five rows, to a width of one foot and two inches. When opening the armhole, decrease one stitch on both sides every other row until the back width is five and a half inches long and one foot wide.

Front panel: Knit 4 inches of ribbing at the edge of the hem. The left lapel has 60 stitches and is also knitted in a window-shaped pattern. The increasing at the waist and armhole decreases are mostly the same as the back. The right lapel is also the same.

Sleeves: Cast on 32 stitches at the shoulder and increase stitches on the left and right sides, increasing one stitch every other row until it is even with the armhole. Use four double-pointed needles to join in a circle. Knit 3 inches of ribbing at the cuff. The second pair of sleeves is the same.

Collar: Use dark yarn to knit a double braid and wrap it around the collar. Sew three buttons at the waist.

Description of Window-Shaped Pattern

Each flower has four stitches, knitted with two colors apart.

First row: Knit one row of knit stitches with dark color.

Second row: Same as the first row.

Third row: Slip one stitch, knit two knit stitches, use light color to knit, slip one stitch, knit two knit stitches.

Fourth row: Slip one stitch, knit two purl stitches, slip one stitch, knit two purl stitches, use light color to knit two purl stitches.

Fifth row: Knit one row of knit stitches, knit with dark color, turn over and still use dark color to knit one row of knit stitches.

Sixth row: Same as the third row, and so on.

An Atomic Flower Jacket by Miss Li Lihua

Briefly Discussing Atomic Flowers

— Songtao

First row: Knit stitch.

Second row: One knit stitch, three knit stitches, knit two stitches together, knit two stitches together, three knit stitches, add one stitch.

Third row: Purl all stitches on the wrong side. Add a stitch where you added a stitch, and knit two stitches together where you knitted two stitches together.

Fourth row: Same as the second row.

Fifth row: Same as the third row.

Sixth row: Same as the second row.

Seventh row: Same as the third row.

Eighth row: Knit two stitches, add one stitch, knit two stitches, knit two stitches together, knit two stitches together, knit two stitches, add one stitch, knit two stitches.

Ninth row: Knit three purl stitches, add one stitch, knit one purl stitch, knit two stitches together (upwards), knit two stitches together, knit one purl stitch, add one stitch, knit three purl stitches.

Tenth row: Knit four knit stitches, add one stitch, knit two stitches together, add one stitch, knit four purl stitches.

Eleventh row: Knit five purl stitches, add one stitch, knit four knit stitches.

Twelfth row: Knit two stitches together, knit three knit stitches, add one stitch, knit one knit stitch, add one stitch, knit three knit stitches, knit three stitches together.

Thirteenth row: Knit two stitches together (upwards), knit three purl stitches, add one stitch, knit one purl stitch, add one stitch, knit three purl stitches.

Fourteenth row: Knit two stitches together, knit three knit stitches, add one stitch, knit one knit stitch, add one stitch, knit three knit stitches.

Fifteenth row: Same as the thirteenth row.

Sixteenth row: Same as the fourteenth row.

Seventeenth row: Same as the thirteenth row.

Eighteenth row: Knit two stitches together, add one stitch, knit three knit stitches, add one stitch, knit two knit stitches.

Nineteenth row: Knit two stitches together, knit one purl stitch, add one stitch, knit three purl stitches, add one stitch, knit one purl stitch, knit two stitches together.

Twentieth row: Knit two stitches together, add one stitch, knit seven purl stitches, add one stitch, knit two stitches together.

Twenty-first row: Knit one knit stitch, add one stitch, knit three knit stitches, add two stitches, knit two stitches together, knit one knit stitch, add one stitch, knit two stitches together, knit three knit stitches, add one stitch, and so on.

A Golden Bellflower Jacket by Kunqu Actress Gao Yuqian

Golden Bellflower Knitting Method

— Feng

Each flower has nine stitches.

First row: Knit stitch.

Second row: Knit three purl stitches, add one stitch, knit one knit stitch, add one stitch, knit three purl stitches.

Third row: Knit three knit stitches, knit three purl stitches, knit three knit stitches.

Fourth row: Knit three purl stitches, add one stitch, knit three knit stitches, add one stitch, knit three purl stitches.

Fifth row: Knit three knit stitches, knit five purl stitches, knit three knit stitches.

Sixth row: Knit three purl stitches, add one stitch, knit five knit stitches, add one stitch, knit three purl stitches.

Seventh row: Knit three knit stitches, knit seven purl stitches, knit three knit stitches.

Eighth row: Knit three purl stitches, add one stitch, knit seven knit stitches, add one stitch, knit three purl stitches.

Ninth row: Knit all stitches in knit stitch.

Tenth row: Knit three purl stitches, wrap each stitch twice, drop them, knit three purl stitches.

Eleventh row: Knit three knit stitches, drop all the wrapped loops one by one, knit three knit stitches.

Twelfth row: Knit three purl stitches, knit nine stitches together, knit three purl stitches.

Thirteenth row: Knit three knit stitches, pick up one horizontal strand and cast it off in a stitch.

Fourteenth row: Same as the second row onwards, and so on.

— Autumn

Knitting art has developed considerably in recent years, partly due to continuous research and partly due to the widespread use of plush materials. Besides being used for coats, vests, and children's clothing, it is also widely used in decorations. This is a cushion woven with a wild chrysanthemum pattern, suitable for sofas, chartered cars, and automobiles, providing a comfortable backrest in all seasons. Not only is the pattern beautiful, but the colors also complement each other, making it elegant and durable. It can also be washed, disassembled, and altered, making it both economical and aesthetically pleasing. Therefore, high-class families generally use this novel cushion to decorate their halls. As for other knitted items such as bedsheets and coarse cloth pillowcases, whether as gifts for relatives and friends or for everyday use, they are both beautiful and unique, and are sure to win praise. Here, we present a model of a domestic cushion for our enthusiasts to use as a reference.

Reunion Moon

— Lü Baihua

A kind of reunion moon, shines on sorrow and shines on joy.

When I received Ying Zikai's

cover painting for the "Free Talk Monthly,"

with these two lines of poetry,

I felt boundless

bewilderment. It's Mid-Autumn Festival again,

the most evocative Mid-Autumn Festival

of the year, especially this

year, this evening, the division

between the levels of sorrow and joy

is even more

profoundly evident.

So, I'm a little tired

of the moon. It is said that the Mid-Autumn Festival moon

is the roundest and brightest. Sun

Fu's poem: "All twelve full moons are

beautiful to see, but the fullest of all is in

Mid-Autumn." Xu Tang's poem: "The power of the moon is

shown every month, but the brightest shine is in

Mid-Autumn." Precisely because under the light of the roundest

and brightest moon, I, who belong

to the sorrowful realm, am

particularly stirred by, or rather,

dissatisfied with reality. Although

the call for thrift resounds through the clouds,

the mooncakes consumed by those seeking pleasure

still rob the poor of a month's

worth of grain, even more so now.

What can be said!

So, I can only simply

fear facing the moon, resent the moon.

Why is it particularly

bright and round during Mid-Autumn? Of course,

the season creates this. The autumn

season is inherently clear, and the autumn colors

are evenly divided tonight, naturally showing the

brightness and roundness of the moon. In the past, Dong

Po heard someone say: "Although Mid-Autumn is tens of thousands

of miles away, one day they will meet and face each other, with the same

weather, whether sunny or cloudy."

It would be strange for the weather to be the same

across tens of thousands of miles. This does not need to be explored. It just

reminds me of Dongpo's "Water Melody," which

is indeed a portrayal of the impoverished class.

The lines "Turns to the vermilion pavilion, lowers to the embroidered door,

shines on the sleepless. There should be no resentment,

why is it rounder at the time of separation."

However, Emperor Shenzong of the Song Dynasty

ordered the singing of this newly popular tune.

"Afraid that the jade towers and mansions,

are unbearable in the high places."

He was so moved that he pardoned his

punishment. Now, how many

people are singing, and how many

are sleepless and resentful? However,

who is moved?

So, the reunion

moon of Mid-Autumn, only when I was a child snuggled

in my mother's arms, pointing

at it with love, I still fear

facing it. I understand that this

relationship is not about the moon, just as Li Lie

wen said in the article he sent me about

Shanghai, "Here I have my

love, and also my hatred and

pain," just as I suspect

that the reunion moon seems to shine particularly on

our poverty and sorrow.

From Autumn to Mid-Autumn

— Wei Zhi

In terms of seasons, I love autumn even more.

Autumn grass in the wind, autumn dew glistening, standing in the morning

by the Yangtze River, looking around blankly, gazing into the distance at the autumn water

the same color as the western sky, I can't help but feel that "wealth to

me is like autumn wind passing through my ears." Emperor Wen of Wei's

poem: "The long autumn night is vast, the fierce north wind is

cold," what a clear and cold realm.

Summer nights are short and unbearable. Autumn nights are getting longer, and mosquitoes are getting fewer.

Place a chair and sit in the garden, looking up at the autumn stars

, which is also quite pleasant. Spring makes people lazy

, summer is full of sweat, and winter can only

close the windows, shut the doors, and lie under the covers. Among the four seasons

, only autumn gives people a sense of clarity and freedom

. George Bernard Shaw said: "People must get used to autumn

." Only by getting used to it can one appreciate the true

beauty of autumn. Among the 19th-century British poets

, Byron was better able to appreciate the desolation of autumn

, while Shelley only admired the splendor of spring

. The reason for this is that Shelley was "inhuman"

, while Byron was too "human"

.

Autumn is the season of harvest, gradually

returning from splendor to simplicity, but it is often the most full

and fulfilling time. From spring to autumn, it is like

a person growing from youth to maturity. Therefore, autumn's

other meaning is "maturity," and beyond this there is a feeling of

twilight. Autumn gentlemen and autumn women, although

they symbolize humanity from splendor to withering, if

they realize that this is inevitable, they can be more

open and free. Huainanzi says: "Spring women think

, autumn gentlemen grieve, and know the transformation of things." This also aligns

with Zhuangzi's views in "Wandering Freely" and "The Equality of Things."

Among the entire three months of autumn, the most

lovable is naturally Mid-Autumn. This is the time when "the weather is cool but not yet cold," most suitable for getting close to nature

. Both the Mid-Autumn Festival and the Double Ninth Festival are good days for enjoyment. Naturally,

in the beginning, the Mid-Autumn Festival had a history of blood and tears

, but as time passed, this day

became a folk festival for "collective enjoyment"

. Today, many villages still have collective activities of small gatherings every three days

and large gatherings every five days, in order to exchange what they have and what they lack, and the so-called "festival"

is just a publicly designated day for collective enjoyment

.

The best flower representing Mid-Autumn is the Osmanthus

, after which comes the Chrysanthemum. Li Shen's poem says: "Chrysanthemums

welcome the autumn festival with urgent west wind," this so-called "autumn festival

" is not the Mid-Autumn Festival, but the Double Ninth Festival.

Just as the Double Ninth Festival has chestnut cakes,

the wonderful product of Mid-Autumn is mooncakes. It is said that this year in Shanghai

the price of a large mooncake is easily over ten thousand

yuan. This, in the eyes of public

employees "all in the west wind," is nothing short of

irony. - The salary adjustment for public

employees in August only added one hundred thousand yuan, which is truly

grateful, a meager large mooncake. The creator of the mooncake was Liu Bowen (Ji

), which is said to contain a history of blood and tears of the Han people under foreign

invasion. "Holding

a steel knife ninety-nine times, killing all the barbarians before stopping."

Such folk songs still seem to linger in the ears.

But to this day, the moon still

shines crookedly on the earth. In the hearts of the big-bellied people or dignitaries who eat big mooncakes, is there

still that bloody memory from more than five hundred years ago

?

Two years since victory, our lives are still far

from the days of "national rejoicing"

. Looking at the current situation in China, and looking ahead

to Japan, which is putting on the facade of "democracy" and burying itself in rapid

advance, we will be even more ashamed.

If those who eat mooncakes think of the history of blood and tears

contained in the mooncakes, can they also feel something?

Autumn is the season of maturity, but China

, when will your fruits of democracy, the fruits of nation-building,

mature?!

Man and Moon Reunion

— Hu Lu

Although it is said that the moon is better in the West, how

can it compare to my Mid-Autumn Festival? Furthermore, burn incense and prepare offerings,

and eat mooncakes, Eastern Divine Land!

Even more miracles, the city celebrates with wine and meat,

while the wilderness is full of skulls! On this joyous reunion festival,

we should be happy and not ask about sorrow!

Osmanthus Palace Autumn

— (Two Verses)

Thinking of the past, resenting the good night, Chang

E's feelings are like the autumn tide, hard to forget Houyi's

bow that bent the moon, deeply afraid that foreign arrows will shoot the sky!

Mourning the end of the kalpa, the chaos of the clan and country, strikes

stop the axe of Wu Gang: the golden wind madly rolls

the laughter of madmen, the jade dew drips for the hungry ghosts!

This Year's Mid-Autumn Festival

— Si Guo

The Mid-Autumn Festival, in small but famous cities like my hometown in Jiangnan,

is a day of excitement for people. Our city has glass-made

"imperial carriages," including all kinds of lamps

, small flags, and small umbrellas. On Mid-Autumn night, all kinds

of lamps are lit, plus fresh pomegranates, water chestnuts,

and mooncakes. The whole family gathers together to pay respect to the Moon Palace,

which is really fun. Parents pay respect to the big Moon

Palace, and children pay respect to the small Moon Palace, everyone rushing

and bustling, very lively.

This was my childhood. At that time, the world

had not fully recognized the continuity and

latent nature of war, and the power of killing and destruction had not

developed to the extent it has now. People, especially

in smaller cities, although constantly trampled

by civil wars, still appreciated the joy of festivals

. Perhaps life had already begun to slightly threaten

my father, but it was not very hideous and terrifying for us children

. We must celebrate the festival like a festival, my mother said

.

The scene at that time, when recalled now

, is both sweet and beautiful: the lamps were so warm

and bright, the light shining from the glass shade in various colors

, twinkling and beautiful and interesting; the mooncakes were so fragrant

and sweet, it seems that people have never been able to make that kind of cake since then

; besides taking out the "imperial carriage" for us to play

with, our parents would also buy many clay figurines and new shoes

for us. Everything was joyous and

wonderful. But now that scene seems to be a historical

relic. When I recall it, there is an unspeakable

melancholy in my heart, a light but deeply sharp melancholy. This is not

just because the beautiful childhood has passed away, because childhood

cannot last forever, but because the peaceful atmosphere of childhood

is no longer there.

Since leaving my hometown, it seems that each year is

worse than the last. The "imperial carriage" has long disappeared

; my parents no longer buy gifts for us on Mid-Autumn Festival

; mooncakes seem to become sweeter and more greasy,

and the so-called lotus seed paste is just sweet potatoes. I started working outside at the age of

seventeen, beginning a bitter life journey

. After the Anti-Japanese War, I suffered in other provinces

. My parents passed away one after another because they were not used to wandering life

. Every year during the Mid-Autumn Festival, I just go through the motions

, and only a sense of indifferent

sadness rises in my heart towards the big, cool, round, and white moon.

What about this year? Logically speaking, returning to my

hometown to celebrate the first Mid-Autumn Festival after victory should be very happy

. But the country is still in turmoil, and I myself am being held tightly

by life, unable to even catch my breath.

I have no heart to enjoy the moon. The little beautiful

childish dreams of the Anti-Japanese War have been awakened

. The world is facing the most terrifying trap

, and one careless step will lead to a fall. Suspicion, hatred, pride, and ignorance

are growing day by day, and everyone understands that

avoiding the next war is not easy.

The worried even shout, "Let's fight it early, an early fight can preserve a part!"

In the past, if A and B had a feud, fighting would settle it whoever lost

; now several groups containing fractions of all mankind each hold a set of

irreconcilable theories, wanting to destroy, if

not to conquer the rest of mankind. The result of this struggle

is hard to imagine, because the two premises of self-defense and defending the

truth do not allow people to let go halfway

. But to this day, no wisdom has emerged to

eliminate people's doubts and strengthen

people's faith in loving others as themselves. Festivals have long been

neglected by people, except for a few extremely rich

or those who never care about the future.

Today, in many small but famous cities

in Jiangnan, the Mid-Autumn Festival still has its irresistible

charm. The sky is clear, and the moon is beautiful

. But people's hearts are heavy. I

can't help but sincerely pray for our generation and the next generation.

Mid-Autumn Festival in America

— Shu Yuan

"The moon is extraordinarily bright at Mid-Autumn," which does not depend on region or nationality. I

have not said that the bright moon is brighter in America than in China. But the same bright moon, in

America, shines on abundant crops, towering factories, prosperous cities, and couples

shoulder to shoulder. In China, it shines on the broken battlefields, the howling of grief across the fields, the hoarded granaries, and the

homeless who sleep in the open air, that light seems more suppressed

. During the eight years of the Anti-Japanese War, I lived in Hengyang and Chengdu for the first four years. Every Mid-Autumn Festival, enemy planes would definitely

arrive to drop bombs, making it impossible to celebrate the festival. In the latter four years, I stayed in the United States, like Su Wu herding sheep, with no interest in

holding chrysanthemums and appreciating the moon. For eight or nine years, there were not many mooncakes imported

. I had hoped to return victorious and enjoy a feast

, but unexpectedly the legal tender depreciated, and mooncakes rose in price. At the same time, there was talk of thrift

, and civil servants did not give or receive gifts. I could not afford to buy them, and no one sent them to me

. "When rituals are lost, seek them among the wild," let's talk about celebrating Mid-Autumn in America:

Overseas Chinese are most interested in celebrating festivals, because they work hard all year round and want to

celebrate the festivals in a lively way. As the Autumn Festival approaches, the Chinese grocery stores

in the major ports of New York and San Francisco are piled high with Cantonese-style mooncakes and incense burners

. Mooncakes are not only bought by Chinese people.

Americans also like to eat Mooncake. Foreign ladies eat mooncakes

and spread and even fabricate many stories about Chang E in the moon

, showing how knowledgeable and up to date they are.

Chinese. Overseas Chinese take a day off on Mid-Autumn Festival, burning incense

in front of the God of Wealth. And making a big scene on the Lantern Festival.

The assembly halls such as the Anliang Hall have a God of Wealth Hall, and are equipped

with a full set of Lantern Festival instruments, gongs and drums, sounding through the sky

. After the Lantern Festival is celebrated, Pai Gow and gambling games

take off, determined to enjoy the day. Cantonese theaters usually post plays such as "Chang E Flies to the Moon,"

but young overseas Chinese prefer to walk arm in arm in the moonlight to the depths of the gardens

, spending their precious time. One year on Mid-Autumn Festival, a young overseas Chinese woman invited me to her home to celebrate the festival

. After drinking and eating my fill, I felt that the moon was especially bright late at night.

Now the situation is very different. Eating Guan Sheng's bread and drinking Chang Tu's wine,

is Mid-Autumn Festival betraying me, or am I betraying Mid-Autumn Festival?

Mid-Autumn Moon

— Xiao Kangshi

This year's Mid-Autumn Moon,

Shows more of separation and chaos!

Because we talk about thrift,

Chang E in the moon does not dance?

The moon is extraordinarily bright at Mid-Autumn, how

many families are separated and chaotic, how many are happy? Today we are talking about thrift

, even affecting Chang E in the moon, who no longer dances!

Note: "Shi Zhou Ji" says that there is

Chang E in the moon, dancing under the osmanthus tree.

Mid-Autumn and Osmanthus

— Yue Feng

"Enjoyable Things" (written by Zhang Yuezai of the Song Dynasty) says, "In August, go to the mountains to find osmanthus, many wonderful

Mountain Osmanthus, Qi Geng Ting Qianye Osmanthus, the painting of Immortals

Building, viewing the Moon and the Osmanthus, climbing the Osmanthus," which shows that

viewing the moon and appreciating the osmanthus are inseparable elegant pastimes

. The connection between the osmanthus and the moon was established long before the Tang Dynasty,

such as when Emperor Chen Hou created the Osmanthus Palace for Zhang Lihua behind the Guangzhao Palace

, making a round door like the moon. In the Tang Dynasty, however, the osmanthus was transplanted to the moon

. Wang Wei's poem, "The osmanthus spirit is first born, and the autumn dew is slight," indicates that at that time

some people had already seen the osmanthus tree in the moon.

Although Wu Gang, who cuts the osmanthus tree, was a Han Chinese, this story

was first seen in the Tang Dynasty's "Miscellaneous Records of Youyang"

, which shows that it was still a creation that harmed people. When Xie Shen wrote his strategies, he called himself a branch of the osmanthus forest

, so the osmanthus tree was intertwined with the autumn examination, simply calling passing the examination

"picking osmanthus."

In modern times, in Yunnan in August, there is an

Osmanthus Flower Market. In Xindu, Sichuan, there is Osmanthus Lake, and the lakeside

has clusters of osmanthus trees, as many as two hundred or more, stretching for a mile

, all hundreds of years old. Around Mid-Autumn Festival, the fragrance

reaches several miles away, and travelers fill the road. In the past, the Wu custom of watching osmanthus

involved the entire city turning out, like a dragon boat race.

The osmanthus flowers of Baozang Temple in Beijing are also very famous

. From this, we can know that the osmanthus tree is commonly planted throughout the north and south of China

. On a bright moonlit night, the swaying shadow of the osmanthus, with strands of sweet fragrance

, talking about family ethics, and spending the festival, is indeed a supreme

pleasure.

When I was a child, I asked my teacher why the

moon revolves around the earth, but we always only see

Wu Gang cutting down the tree (this is the view of the Jiahu area), and not see

the other sides of the moon.

That teacher was truly knowledgeable. He said that when the moon

revolves around the earth, it is also rotating itself at the same time

, just like the earth revolving around the sun. The only

difference is that the moon's rotation time is exactly

one lunar month, which is equal to the time it takes to revolve around the earth

once. Therefore, although it keeps

revolving around the earth, it always only lets us

see the side with Wu Gang and the osmanthus tree.

As for what happened after Wu Gang cut down the tree, whether Wu Gang had

a wife and children, etc., it would not let us

see. I say that teacher was knowledgeable

, because he was an elementary school teacher thirty years ago

. I later talked about this question with many geography teachers and friends

, and they all said they had not paid attention to it.

The Story of Mid-Autumn

— Han Xiao

Time seems to pass especially fast, and in the

blink of an eye, it's Mid-Autumn Festival again.

Speaking of Mid-Autumn, one can't help but think

of the Mid-Autumn moon. In China, there are many bizarre

legends about the Mid-Autumn moon. Let the author

write two paragraphs below as gifts to commemorate the Mid-Autumn Festival

.

Chang E Flies to the Moon According to legend, more than four thousand years

ago, in the Xia Dynasty, Houyi assisted Emperor Xiang in governing the country

, and begged the Queen Mother of the West for the elixir of immortality. His wife Chang

E (also called Heng E) stole it and fled to the moon. In this way, she would

live forever and dwell permanently on

the moon. The people have adapted her into a play, which

must be performed on stage every festival.

The Old Man Under the Moon Some people believe that there is

a jade rabbit in the moon. In Buddhism, it is also believed that

that rabbit was a devout Buddhist who voluntarily sacrificed

his lifelong happiness for the sake of the Bodhisattva. Heaven, in order to reward

its loyalty, made it

reborn, and thus became the Old Man Under the Moon. This old man

shoulders all the missions of the moon god, especially

promoting the marriage of lovers. So to this day,

there are still many superstitious and loving women who

cut white paper into the shape of rabbits on Mid-Autumn Day

and place them inside their daughters' shoes. They believe that

their daughters will soon be able to choose

a satisfactory husband and thus marry and live to old age together

.

When the Moon is Full

— Wei Zhuang

Zhu Renkong Pingzhong's moon-viewing poem says: "The round ice mirror emits pure splendor

, is tonight like last night? I only fear that the moonlight has no likes or dislikes, but pity that people's hearts

have fullness and emptiness."

We always feel that the moon of Mid-Autumn is particularly full

and exceptionally bright, so moon-viewing must be on Mid-Autumn night.

In fact, on the fourteenth, although there is still a line of incompleteness

, as far as our naked eyes can see, we already feel that it is very full

. And on the sixteenth, in fact, Mid-Autumn has long passed

, but when you look up at the bright moon, who can distinguish where it is incomplete

? After the sixteenth, it should be discussed separately.

We always have endless hope for the future

, believing that everything can be as ideal as possible; we also

tend to have feelings of nostalgia and sentimentality for everything in the past

. Until things have passed and circumstances have changed, as if the moon has already waned

, looking back at the scene of the waxing crescent, reminiscing

about the past, it instead increases many beautiful memories

!

The so-called "moonlight has no likes or dislikes, and people's hearts have fullness and emptiness." Everything in the universe is not

absolute. If we can think one step back, we will naturally have endless joy

, while deliberately seeking perfection and being endlessly greedy

often only results in grasping an empty black shadow.

Lao Tzu said: "Holding to fullness is not as good as stopping; sharpening to sharpness cannot be long preserved. Gold and jade fill the hall, but none can keep them; wealth and nobility with pride invite their own blame. To retire when the task is accomplished is the Way of Heaven."

In all things under heaven, when things reach an extreme, they will be reversed; when prosperity reaches its peak, it will decline, and when adversity reaches its end, prosperity will come. But if you can often see a crescent moon, you can have endless hope. By the twelfth or thirteenth day, you will gradually have the intention of splendor. As for after the sixteenth, the day is eclipsed, and how can you hide it?

Maintaining fullness and preserving stability is an old saying, but retreating bravely in the face of a raging current is still considered a wise move. Do moon-viewers have this intention?

Autumn Night Moon

— Sun Yuehan

Mid-Autumn Festival. Clear and long sky,

congealed dewdrops, constrained liver yang. Calculating material prices,

trivial matters of rice and salt. How

many things, occasionally recalling, old sorrows are difficult to stop

. Passive; the heart's screen will not be lifted tonight.

Friends and relatives are far away, working as expatriates,

like prodigal sons, all extravagance is buttoned up. Past

romantic dreams, melting ice and snow, leaving

mountains and rivers (or hometown), all broken

. Desolate and sad. Afraid to look at the exquisite

round moon late at night.

Old Customs of the Mid-Autumn Festival

— Xiang Ruo

Mid-Autumn, commonly known as the Eighth Month Half, on this evening, families each have

banquets to celebrate the festival. People also use the weather of this night to predict

the weather of the next Lantern Festival, saying, "If clouds cover the moon on the fifteenth of the eighth month,

next year's Lantern Festival will be rained on." It is also said: "Rain beats the Lantern Festival lights, clouds

cover the Mid-Autumn moon." Cai Yun's poem says: "Heart heavy, Mid-Autumn clouds cover the moon,

at dawn, Lantern Festival clothes are drenched by rain, who knows when the bean flowers bloom,

nurturing rice is just right with water overflowing." Thus, the interests of farmers and the leisurely

are indeed quite different. Zhou Gong's collection has the line, "I only wish not to see the moon during Mid-Autumn,

to get rain beating the Lantern Festival lights," truly the words of a benevolent man. However, for elegant scholars who enjoy watching the moon and appreciating lanterns, wouldn't they consider this

"too much of a buzzkill?"

On the evening of Mid-Autumn, every household has flower arrangements and fragrant candles, worshipping towards the sky:

Children kowtow under the moon, playing in front of the lanterns, called worshiping the moon palace. Lu Qi's Beijing Annual Customs records: "On the evening of Mid-Autumn,

families each set up an image of the moon palace talisman, with a rabbit standing like a human on the talisman.

Fruits and melons are placed in the courtyard, and the cake surface is painted with a toad and rabbit in the moon. Men and women respectfully worship and burn incense,

and then burn it." Now, it is not customary to set up images of moon palace talismans, only to worship towards the sky.

In Wu customs, there is also the burning of incense buckets. Incense shops make buckets with incense sticks,

and fill them with incense powder. Monks and laypeople alike buy them, burning them under the moon.

You Songzhen's poem on incense buckets says: "Picking up incense threads, evenly and finely,

making them into the same shape as a bucket, only suitable for spiritual sandalwood mixed with wood shavings,

how could fine wine be stored in the jade palace, beautiful women lower the curtains and bend their waists frequently,

scholars read the stars and leave the handle empty, Wu customs pass on elegant stories during Mid-Autumn,

the fragrant osmanthus fills the courtyard, right in the wind."

Another poem says: "Ashamed I have no beautiful verses to collect mountain fragrance, talent and thought are difficult to measure this thing,

candle flames rush up, spearing through the moon, the sandalwood core sinks, like a gallbladder in a bag,

the smoke still forms delicate examination essays, the ashes still leave a square seal pattern, if a group of

true immortals descends to the mortal realm late at night, they would not mind singing rainbow skirts in a small room." In Hangzhou customs, they

paste paper to make a bucket, burning incense inside. The tall ones can be about two feet high. Wu Manyun's poem says: "The heart character burns to the end, inch by inch ashes, spiritual incense asks the moon wheel to open:

what the bucket measures is ultimately little in the human world, freshly harvested osmanthus grains are ten thousand bushels."

Women dress up and go out to play, visiting each other, or following along to temples as they please.

The rooster crows, yet they still dance under the moon, called walking the moonlight.

Cai Yun's poem says: "Osmanthus flower balls press down on silk fragrance, in twos and threes, sisters walk,

walking in the cold, not minding the thin silk sleeves, on the road they hate that their skirts are too long."

Villagers in the wilderness stack tiles to form a seven-story pagoda, with

an image of Ksitigarbha in the middle, lit with lamps all around, called pagoda lamps. This is meant to

illuminate the underworld, not just for sightseeing. Mei Shuangyai's poem says:

"No need to reduce the rammed earth layers, one pillar supporting the sky, seven levels of lights, the bronze sparrow terrace ashes leave pieces,

the spiritual light palace gravel accumulates layers, the candle dragon scales rush up to the sky palace, the toad pearls rise from the ground,

gentlemen and ladies pour out of the city, standing and watching, the rice star and bright moon increase the scenery even more."

Families give mooncakes as Mid-Autumn Festival gifts. On the fifteenth night,

they arrange fruits and melons to offer before the moon-worshiping feast. Qi Qi's poem says:

"Mid-Autumn Festival gifts are not cheap, fire stoves are busy, fresh from the pot,

the same cake makers have newly made, good names are first written toward the moon." The West Lake Travelogue records: "During Mid-Autumn, the common people give each other mooncakes,

taking the meaning of reunion." Wu Manyun's Jiangxiang Festival Objects poem preface:

"Hangzhou customs eat mooncakes during Mid-Autumn, setting up a moon-worshiping feast at night, taking the meaning of human and moon becoming

round." The poem says: "Powdered cream, round shadow, the moon divides its light, not

red silk, yet one eats to be full, only fearing that the reunion is empty talk on the cake, how many soldiers

have not yet returned home." This poem, even if moved to today, is very relevant.

Mooncakes come in many styles, with the more expensive ones selling for millions, with painted

figures and a hundred scenes on the surface, decorated gorgeously, the common people look at them like the moon palace,

unable to immediately obtain them. After the victory, atomic mooncakes were prevalent on the market,

I wonder if there will be flying saucer mooncakes appearing this autumn.

Feelings on the Mid-Autumn Festival of the Thirty-Sixth Year

— Bao Zaizi

The occupied area is still not recovered, already two weeks. The local

evolution, the atmosphere is bleak. Rain and dew, thunder, and advancement are out of sync,

bandits and the smoke of war arise everywhere. People's hearts are unpredictable, families

drift and scatter. Restraining oneself and waiting, eyes looking for the dawn to break.

Scratching my head and asking the sky, my heart is alarmed by the red flames flying.

Looking around the realm, snakes and dragons compete, chickens and dogs are not peaceful.

I only see crows everywhere, cawing randomly into the wind.

It will be published soon, and it is hoped that readers will pay attention.

As for the author of "American Miscellany," he will be publishing a separate book, and it is planned to temporarily end this section.
